Important Update: Mandatory Withdrawals for UK Stakeholder Pensions Under UK pension regulations, individuals aged 75 and over must begin drawing down their stakeholder pension funds or transfer them to a drawdown plan. The deadline for first withdrawals is the end of the tax year in which you turn 75. If you’re unsure whether your account qualifies, please contact our client services team with your scheme reference number. We’ve attached a step-by-step guide in PDF format for your convenience. This is not optional under HMRC rules.
